
            INSERT INTO dara_mallas_specialization_major
                (
                    name,
                    "number",
                    code,
                    specialization_id,
                    saes_code_id,
                    company_id
                )
                SELECT
                    'L602' AS name,
                    0 AS "number",
                    0 AS code,
                    s.id AS specialization_id,
                    sc.id AS saes_code_id,
                    3 AS company_id
                FROM dara_mallas_specialization s
                JOIN dara_mallas_program p
                    ON p.id = s.program_id
                    AND p.name = 'GESTION EN SALUD OCUPACIONAL Y AMBIENTE'
                    AND p.description = 'TÉCNICO EN GESTIÓN EN SALUD OCUPACIONAL Y AMBIENTE'
                    AND p.period_id = (
                        SELECT id
                        FROM dara_mallas_period
                        WHERE name = '000000'
                        AND company_id = 3
                    )
                    AND p.company_id = 3
                JOIN dara_mallas_saes_code sc
                    ON sc.name = 'L602'
                    AND sc.company_id = 3
                WHERE s.company_id = 3
                AND NOT EXISTS (
                    SELECT 1
                    FROM dara_mallas_specialization_major sm
                    WHERE sm.name = 'L602'
                    AND sm.specialization_id = s.id
                    AND sm.saes_code_id = sc.id
                    AND sm.company_id = 3
                );

                    3 AS company_id
                FROM dara_mallas_specialization s
                JOIN dara_mallas_program p
                    ON p.id = s.program_id
                    AND p.name = 'INGENIERÍA ELECTRÓNICA EN TELECOMUNICACIONES'
                    AND p.description = 'LICENCIATURA EN INGENIERÍA ELECTRÓNICA EN TELECOMUNICACIONES'
                    AND p.period_id = (
                        SELECT id
                        FROM dara_mallas_period
                        WHERE name = '000000'
                        AND company_id = 3
                    )
                    AND p.company_id = 3
                JOIN dara_mallas_saes_code sc
                    ON sc.name = '237'
                    AND sc.company_id = 3
                WHERE s.company_id = 3
                AND NOT EXISTS (

                    FROM dara_mallas_specialization_major sm
                    WHERE sm.name = '237'
                    AND sm.specialization_id = s.id
                    AND sm.saes_code_id = sc.id
                    AND sm.company_id = 3
                );

                    "number",
                    code,
                    specialization_id,
                    saes_code_id,
                    company_id
                )
                SELECT
                    '457' AS name,
                    0 AS "number",
                    0 AS code,
                    s.id AS specialization_id,
                    sc.id AS saes_code_id,
                    3 AS company_id
                FROM dara_mallas_specialization s
                JOIN dara_mallas_program p
                    ON p.id = s.program_id
                    AND p.name = 'COMUNICACION Y MERCADEO'
                    AND p.description = 'MAESTRIA PROFESIONAL EN COMUNICACION Y MERCADEO'
                    AND p.period_id = (
                        SELECT id
                        FROM dara_mallas_period
                        WHERE name = '000000'
                        AND company_id = 3
                    )
                    AND p.company_id = 3
                JOIN dara_mallas_saes_code sc
                    ON sc.name = '457'
                    AND sc.company_id = 3
                WHERE s.company_id = 3
                AND NOT EXISTS (
                    SELECT 1
                    FROM dara_mallas_specialization_major sm
                    WHERE sm.name = '457'
                    AND sm.specialization_id = s.id
                    AND sm.saes_code_id = sc.id
                    AND sm.company_id = 3
                );

                    AND p.name = 'TECNOLOGÍAS DE LA INFORMACIÓN PARA LA GESTIÓN DE LOS NEGOCIOS'
                    AND p.description = 'LICENCIATURA EN TECNOLOGÍAS DE LA INFORMACIÓN PARA LA GESTIÓN DE LOS NEGOCIOS'
                    AND p.period_id = (
                        SELECT id
                        FROM dara_mallas_period
                        WHERE name = '000000'
                        AND company_id = 3
                    )
                    AND p.company_id = 3
                JOIN dara_mallas_saes_code sc
                    ON sc.name = '242'
                    AND sc.company_id = 3
                WHERE s.company_id = 3
                AND NOT EXISTS (
                    SELECT 1
                    FROM dara_mallas_specialization_major sm
                    WHERE sm.name = '242'
                    AND sm.specialization_id = s.id
                    AND sm.saes_code_id = sc.id
                    AND sm.company_id = 3
                );

                    saes_code_id,
                    company_id
                )
                SELECT
                    'A462' AS name,
                    0 AS "number",
                    0 AS code,
                    s.id AS specialization_id,
                    sc.id AS saes_code_id,
                    3 AS company_id
                FROM dara_mallas_specialization s
                JOIN dara_mallas_program p
                    ON p.id = s.program_id
                    AND p.name = 'ADMINISTRACION DE NEGOCIOS CON ENFASIS EN GERENCIA'
                    AND p.description = 'MAESTRIA EN ADMINISTRACION DE NEGOCIOS CON ENFASIS EN GERENCIA'
                    AND p.period_id = (
                        SELECT id
                        FROM dara_mallas_period
                        WHERE name = '000000'
                        AND company_id = 3
                    )
                    AND p.company_id = 3
                JOIN dara_mallas_saes_code sc
                    ON sc.name = 'A462'
                    AND sc.company_id = 3
                WHERE s.company_id = 3
                AND NOT EXISTS (
                    SELECT 1
                    FROM dara_mallas_specialization_major sm
                    WHERE sm.name = 'A462'
                    AND sm.specialization_id = s.id
                    AND sm.saes_code_id = sc.id
                    AND sm.company_id = 3
                );
